               DataItemTable=Table15;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               RESET;
                               SETFILTER("No.",AccountNo);
                               B1:=TRUE;
                               B2:=TRUE;
                               B3:=TRUE;
                               CASE JournalFormat OF
                                JournalFormat::Bank:  BEGIN
                                  IF Sumup THEN
                                    ReportTitle := Text008
                                  ELSE
                                    ReportTitle := Text009;
                                    B1:=FALSE;        END;
                                JournalFormat::Cash:  BEGIN
                                  IF Sumup THEN
                                    ReportTitle := Text010
                                  ELSE
                                    ReportTitle := Text011;
                                    B2:=FALSE;     END;
                                JournalFormat::AR: BEGIN
                                  IF Sumup THEN
                                    ReportTitle := Text012
                                  ELSE
                                    ReportTitle := Text013;
                                    B3:=FALSE;     END;
                                JournalFormat::AP:  BEGIN
                                  IF Sumup THEN
                                    ReportTitle := Text014
                                  ELSE
                                    ReportTitle := Text015;
                                    B3:=FALSE;     END;
                                JournalFormat::Expense:  BEGIN
                                  IF Sumup THEN
                                    ReportTitle := Text016
                                  ELSE
                                    ReportTitle := Text017;
                                    B3:=FALSE;     END;
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  GLAccount.RESET;
                                  GLAccount.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
                                  IF DateBegin <> 0D THEN
                                    GLAccount.SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,CALCDATE('-1D',DateBegin));
                                  IF GLAccount.FIND('-') THEN
                                    GLAccount.CALCFIELDS("Net Change");

                                  CurrentlyBalance := GLAccount."Net Change";
                                END;
                                 }

                             CHS=由期间];

                             CLEAR(AccountingPeriods);

                             AccountingPeriods.LOOKUPMODE := TRUE;
                             IF AccountingPeriods.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                               AccountingPeriods.GETRECORD(AccountPeriod);
                               DateBegin := AccountPeriod."Starting Date";
                             END;
                           END;
                            }

      { 1000000003;2;Field  ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=End Period;
                             CHS=至期间];
                  SourceExpr=DateEnd;
                  TableRelation="Accounting Period"."Starting Date";
                  OnLookup=BEGIN

                             CLEAR(AccountingPeriods1);
                             AccountingPeriods1.EDITABLE := FALSE;
                             AccountingPeriods1.LOOKUPMODE := TRUE;
                             IF AccountingPeriods1.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                               AccountingPeriods1.GETRECORD(AccountPeriod);
                               DateEnd := CALCDATE('-1D',AccountPeriod."Starting Date");
                             END;
                           END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function GetDirection(ByVal Value As Decimal, ByVal DR As String, ByVal CR As String)
  if Value &gt;0
     Return DR
  else
     if Value &lt; 0
       Return CR
      else
        Return  ""
     end if
  end if
End Function

Public Function FormatNumbers(ByVal Value)
  if Value = 0
    Return ""
  else
    Return FormatNumber(Value)
  end if
End Function

Shared TotalBalance As Decimal
Shared TotalDebit As Decimal
Shared TotalCredit As Decimal
Public Function CalcAmount(ByVal Balance As Decimal,ByVal Debit As Decimal,ByVal Credit As Decimal)
  TotalDebit += Debit
  TotalCredit += Credit
  TotalBalance += Debit - Credit
  Return Balance
End Function

Public Function GetBalance()
  Return TotalBalance
End Function  

Public Function GetDebit()
  Return TotalDebit
End Function  

Public Function GetCredit()
  Return TotalCredit
End Function  

Shared ReportTitle_H1 As String
Shared ReportTitle_H2 As String
Shared ReportTitle_H3 As String
Public Function SetReportTitle(ByVal Parm1 As String,ByVal Parm2 As String,ByVal Parm3 As String)
